## Container | DreamHack 2014 Dust II Souvenir Package (id: 9156)

### Item Changes

  possibleSouvenirStickers: [
    1963,
    1964,
    1965,

    1968,

    1992,

    1998,

    2002,

    2005,

    2007,
    2008,
    2009,
    2010,
    2011,
    2012,
    2013,
    2072,
    2073,
    2074,
    2075,
    2076,
    2077,
    2078,
    2079,
    2080,
    2081,
    2082,
